    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app',

  <span id="freeText13367043989487156885" style="display:none"><b>Debut romance author, Sarah Robinson, arrives with her first book in a new romantic suspense series, The Photographer Trilogy, sure to keep fans of thrillers and romance on the edge of their seats. </b><br /><br />A woman haunted by her past, Kate Jackson was listlessly floating through life until she meets charming lawyer and play boy, Derrick Kane. Just when she thinks she might have found the key to learning how to live again, learning how to love…The Photographer rips it all away with one click of his camera. <br /><br />He takes a picture of every woman he kills. A little memento of his favorite moments. The infamous serial killer is on the attack, but little did Kate know that death could be the one thing to bring her back to life. <br /><br />Or that The Photographer is just beginning… <br /><br /><i>Trigger Warning: Due to violent and dark subject matter, this book is intended for 18+ years old. This book does contain triggers for violence and abuse. This is the first book in a trilogy and ends on a cliffhanger. The next book, Tainted Pictures, is available on all retailers. </i></span>

<div id="review_1178007003" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1178007003" />
    <a title="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict"><img alt="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551124421p2/10717098.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1178007003?book_show_action=true">Jan 23, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" href="/user/show/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict">Carol [Goodreads Addict]</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=mystery">mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=suspense">suspense</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1178007003" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5982043848077361768"><a href='http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/10013222_10202830245831300_1214969173_n1_zpsmbw9h6ov.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423710032i/13661755._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo 10013222_10202830245831300_1214969173_n1_zpsmbw9h6ov.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Tainted Bodies is book one in the Photographer Trilogy by Sarah Robinson. <br/><br/><b>
  <i>“The world might be tainted, but we don’t have to be.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>Kate Jackson has not had an easy life. After an unthinkable violation when she was just a child, her mother left and her father slowly drank himself to death. So Kate and her little sister Annie were all each other had left. Their bond as sisters was unbreakable. Her life as an adult is definitely not what she envisioned for herself. She is working at an office </span>
  <span id="freeText5982043848077361768" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/10013222_10202830245831300_1214969173_n1_zpsmbw9h6ov.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423710032i/13661755._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 10013222_10202830245831300_1214969173_n1_zpsmbw9h6ov.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Tainted Bodies is book one in the Photographer Trilogy by Sarah Robinson. <br><br><b>
  <i>“The world might be tainted, but we don’t have to be.”</i>
</b><br><br>Kate Jackson has not had an easy life. After an unthinkable violation when she was just a child, her mother left and her father slowly drank himself to death. So Kate and her little sister Annie were all each other had left. Their bond as sisters was unbreakable. Her life as an adult is definitely not what she envisioned for herself. She is working at an office furniture store. It’s not her dream job but it’s paying the bills. <br><br>It’s on her way to work one morning at her favorite coffee shop that a chance meeting with the oh so handsome lawyer, Derrick Kane, changes her life. She immediately feels that little spark of attraction with Derrick. Their courtship isn’t rushed but for her she knows that he could be something special. Maybe even the one!<br><br>Derrick Kane is falling in love with Kate. The more time they spend together the stronger his feelings are for her. But Derrick has secrets of his own. Secrets that prevent him from committing fully to any woman, even Kate Jackson. But is he willing to risk losing Kate to protect himself? Or is it maybe time to give his trust and his heart to this woman?<br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/Rapevictims-300x200_zpsmallubgz.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423710032i/13661756.jpg" alt=" photo Rapevictims-300x200_zpsmallubgz.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Just when they are finally able to take their relationship to the next level, neither of them ever feeling happier, the unthinkable happens. Kate’s life is forever changed. And the chance for happiness with Derrick seems to disintegrate right before her eyes. <br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/Woman-leaning-against-door-frame-CBP1012836_zpsk1fxs139.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423710032i/13661757._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo Woman-leaning-against-door-frame-CBP1012836_zpsk1fxs139.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>First I want to say that this series is based on real events. It does contain delicate subject matter that may be upsetting to some. The description of the one violent scene is very tastefully done. I thought Sarah did a wonderful job with this and with allowing us to understand what was going on in Kate’s mind during and after this event. <br><br>At times I thought that too much time was spent dwelling on Kate and Derrick’s relationship as it progressed but I do understand that it was important to the story line to experience their relationship as it slowly grew stronger. <br><br>Even though Kate is making some mistakes dealing with this situation, I have to say I am as proud of her as if she were my own. That woman has more backbone in her pinkie finger than most of us ever will in our whole bodies. Is Kate still in danger? Will her relationship with Derrick survive? I can’t wait to continue on with this trilogy to see what happens next.<br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/12763610_zps6i7fuxrg.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423710032i/13661758.jpg" alt=" photo 12763610_zps6i7fuxrg.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_1185745627" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1185745627" />
    <a title="Pam" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13865261-pam"><img alt="Pam" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1374039144p2/13865261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1185745627?book_show_action=true">Jan 30, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pam" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pam" href="/user/show/13865261-pam">Pam</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=fucked-up-n-broken">fucked-up-n-broken</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=darkerside-mindfuckery">darkerside-mindfuckery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=suspense-chills-n-thrills">suspense-chills-n-thrills</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=3">3</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=mystery-kinda-luv">mystery-kinda-luv</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1185745627" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5532370333583241185"><i>3.5 tainted stars</i><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>It felt like a painting of perfection hiding secrets behind its facade.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422680323i/13534131._SY540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/> <br/><b><u>Note from the author:</u> <i>People are hurt. People are killed. People make mistakes, one that will have you screaming at your e-reader with rage, maybe even disgust. I ask you to go into this story with an open mind, because this is based on a true story.</i></b><br/><br/>I had to include the note from the author in my review, because it was a good reminder for me because when I finished the book, I pretty much was in </span>
  <span id="freeText5532370333583241185" style="display:none"><i>3.5 tainted stars</i><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>It felt like a painting of perfection hiding secrets behind its facade.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422680323i/13534131._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><b><u>Note from the author:</u> <i>People are hurt. People are killed. People make mistakes, one that will have you screaming at your e-reader with rage, maybe even disgust. I ask you to go into this story with an open mind, because this is based on a true story.</i></b><br><br>I had to include the note from the author in my review, because it was a good reminder for me because when I finished the book, I pretty much was in a bad state and didn't know if I wanted to continue on. Then after I talked it out, I realized how I could even judge a book that was based on a true story, it's not like the story could change, because if it did that would make it fiction. <br><br>I found it hard to remember that I'm not reading one of my fairy tales, that in real life, people don't have the slightest clue what to do or how to act in difficult situations. It's the fact that I am reminded of how ugly our society can be that gets me depressed, (a reason why I don't watch the news). Try as I might that to believe that I would know what to do and what to say, I know deep down that I am full of shit, I'd probably react just like everyone in the book... Watching it all unravel and just go from bad to worse, was a hard pill to swallow. <br><br>With that said, this is Kate's story, <b>Tainted Bodies</b> is a story I wouldn't wish upon my worst enemy. It was a slow build, getting a feel of who Kate is now, hints of her past and the event that would change her life forever. I was left, upset and mad, wondering how so much bad can happen to one person and thank my guardian angel for watching over me. <br><br>And now to explain my 3.5 rating, mind you this has nothing to do with the story, it was more how the story was told to me versus inviting me to live in the story with them. I'm not sure if that would makes sense to most, but it's the best way I can describe it. <br><br>The author, thank god for her and how she humbly and graciously put up with me and my initial rant, gave me a little insight. This was one of the very first stories she has ever written, and over time people grow into their trade and evolve, this is one of those series. We will see the progression of not only how the characters grow but the author's style as well as Kate's story is told in three books. I may not have jumped into the second book right away but I had to sort through my thoughts and put things back into perspective in order for me to continue; wishing and hoping that something good will happen for Kate. <br><br><i>ARC kindly provided by the author, in exchange for an honest review.</i><br> <br>***Quotes above are taken from the ARC version of the book and may differ upon publication.<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="5532370333583241185" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_912668949" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/912668949" />
    <a title="Jessica  (Angie &amp; Jessica&#39;s Dreamy Reads)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7530032-jessica-angie-jessica-s-dreamy-reads"><img alt="Jessica  (Angie &amp; Jessica&#39;s Dreamy Reads)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1508375424p2/7530032.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/912668949?book_show_action=true">Apr 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica  (Angie &amp; Jessica&#39;s Dreamy Reads)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica  (Angie &amp; Jessica&#39;s Dreamy Reads)" href="/user/show/7530032-jessica-angie-jessica-s-dreamy-reads">Jessica  (Angie &amp; Jessica&#39;s Dreamy Reads)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer912668949" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10312098720430195103"><strong>Didn't work. (Minor spoilers)</strong><br/><br/>It's never fun to review a book poorly, but I'm a firm believer in honesty, so I'll try to explain.<br/><br/>The first 50% of this book was nothing but dates, cheesy flirtation and coffee. I needed a little bit more meat in my story to keep me interested. The story and the characters felt very under developed. I had nothing to connect me to these characters, nothing to keep me invested in their stories. It was just very bland. I don't know if this is a debut novel by this auth</span>
  <span id="freeText10312098720430195103" style="display:none"><strong>Didn't work. (Minor spoilers)</strong><br /><br />It's never fun to review a book poorly, but I'm a firm believer in honesty, so I'll try to explain.<br /><br />The first 50% of this book was nothing but dates, cheesy flirtation and coffee. I needed a little bit more meat in my story to keep me interested. The story and the characters felt very under developed. I had nothing to connect me to these characters, nothing to keep me invested in their stories. It was just very bland. I don't know if this is a debut novel by this author or not, but this book read like the author is still trying to get her footing in her writing. It wasn't fluid, it was choppy. The dialogue was stiff and forced, it didn't come naturally at all. It didn't feel like conversation two young people would have with each other.<br /><br />I also found it a tad inconsistent. Derek is declaring his love for Kate after what seemed like two dates, but four months later they're not exclusive, he doesn't want to put a label on it? Kate repeatedly declares that they spend every waking moment together, yet Derek won't commit. Six months in, they're on vacation together, and she pretty much had to talk him into calling her his girlfriend. It came off as incredibly pathetic, and I almost shut the book right there. It didn't jive. I sort of stopped committing to this story early on because it lacked believability. And it made the main female character look extremely weak... It's really hard to connect to a weak character or to invest in her story.<br /><br />*Spoiler*<br />I had a really difficult time with Kate's behavior after she was attacked. She was infuriated that no one believed her when she told her parents about the abuse she endured as a child, that the perpetrator got away with it. Yet, now as an adult, she's attacked again, and refuses to speak to the police? And then Derek discovers what happened to her and leaves for a meeting? I mean, come on!! No one acts that way! This whole scenario further cemented the fact that the characters and their personalities were seriously inconsistent and underdeveloped. The story lacked any real depth and the whole thing was poorly delivered.<br /><br />I read somewhere that this book would please readers who enjoy a good episode of Law and Order SVU... unfortunately, I never drew that connection. It actually read more like a cheesy sitcom with some minor drama thrown in. It's supposed to me suspenseful, but I felt no suspense.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10312098720430195103" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer4482737484222431349"><b>
  <i>Tainted Bodies</i>
</b> was surprisingly a really good read in my book! I normally don’t like anything with law and crime since my dad has been a police officer all of my life and have therefore overheard a lot of stories regarding these topics so I was pretty reluctant to read this but am glad I did anyway.<br/><br/>What actually ended up snatching me was the scorching chemistry and connection between Kate and Derrick.   <span id="freeText4482737484222431349" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>Tainted Bodies</i>
</b> was surprisingly a really good read in my book! I normally don’t like anything with law and crime since my dad has been a police officer all of my life and have therefore overheard a lot of stories regarding these topics so I was pretty reluctant to read this but am glad I did anyway.<br /><br />What actually ended up snatching me was the scorching chemistry and connection between Kate and Derrick. I liked how they are both tainted and broken in their own ways. Meaning, none of them is necessarily perfect and have flaws. I thought they were super cute as a couple until one wrench is thrown into the story and left me really NOT liking Derrick. It was pretty unexpected and not the reaction I was hoping from him. Nuh uh. Would I have taken him back after that? Heck no!!<br />I got upset when Kate got hurt. Especially when it had to do with the horrible crime that was committed against her and then Derrick being a letdown. <br /> <br />Btw, the ending really gutted me and was a real cliffhanger!! Really left me hanging with my emotions all over the floor!! I can’t wait for book two now!!<br /><br />Will Kate be able to survive? Will she and Derrick be able to keep it together to find the truth behind the crime? <br /><br />Read and you will find out!! I can't wait for book two!!</span>

<div id="review_903263358" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/903263358" />
    <a title="Christina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13537995-christina"><img alt="Christina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1515001191p2/13537995.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/903263358?book_show_action=true">Apr 06, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christina" href="/user/show/13537995-christina">Christina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13537995-christina?shelf=reviewed-2014">reviewed-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer903263358" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7224842754010935999">Kate graduated near the top of her class with a degree in Psychology, but after graduation she finds herself working in office furniture sales, a far cry from the field she had spent the last four years studying. She seems to be simply going through the motions of life, just trying to put food on the table, until she meets a charismatic stranger, Derrick, at her local coffee shop. The two hit it off right away and soon they find themselves spending all of their spare time with each other.<br/><br/>Derrick</span>
  <span id="freeText7224842754010935999" style="display:none">Kate graduated near the top of her class with a degree in Psychology, but after graduation she finds herself working in office furniture sales, a far cry from the field she had spent the last four years studying. She seems to be simply going through the motions of life, just trying to put food on the table, until she meets a charismatic stranger, Derrick, at her local coffee shop. The two hit it off right away and soon they find themselves spending all of their spare time with each other.<br /><br />Derrick is fresh out of law school and is working at a local firm when he strikes up a conversation, in a most unusual way, with Kate. He is immediately drawn to her and after months of courtship, he finds himself confronting ghosts from is past that are keeping him from committing himself completely to Kate. Kate wants more from the relationship than Derrick is willing to give, but when faced with the prospect of losing her, is he willing to take a chance and find happiness once and for all? When tragedy strikes, Kate &amp; Derrick soon find themselves fighting for more than just the love they share together. They will soon fight for answers and justice, so that together they can find their happily ever after, together.<br /><br />Tainted Bodies is a well-written, well developed, page turning thriller. From the very beginning we are introduced to characters that are slightly broken, but are working hard to mend themselves. The characters are interesting, yet seem to each hold secrets that keep the reader engaged with the knowledge that there will be more divulged, without showing all of their cards at once. The storyline is intelligent and well paced, with just enough twists and turns to keep the reader engaged, while still being plausible.<br /><br />Tainted Bodies is a solid four and a half star read. My only knock was the ending. I’m really not a fan of the cliffhanger ending and in this case it almost felt like hitting the pause button just a little too soon, it felt that there could possibly be a little more resolution in the book, especially considering the way the book starts with the prologue (the prologue is present day, the book is essentially telling the story up to that point). I will definitely be around for the next volume, Tainted Pictures, which will be released later this month! <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7224842754010935999" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_872518782" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/872518782" />
    <a title="C.M. Foss" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17402767-c-m-foss"><img alt="C.M. Foss" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442980031p2/17402767.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/872518782?book_show_action=true">Mar 05, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="C.M. Foss" class="user" itemprop="url" name="C.M. Foss" href="/user/show/17402767-c-m-foss">C.M. Foss</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer872518782" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6747105205675028035">Oh my goodness I loved this book for so many reasons!<br/>You can tell the author took her time writing it, because the characters are well developed and there's an in depth and intricate (not convoluted) plot. I haven't read a crime/law type romance novel in a long time, and I'd forgotten just how much I love them! So all this to say, first off, I loved the story and the way it's written.<br/>But what I really really REALLY loved was how real it was!! I'm weird. I want romance, I want suspense, I want ho</span>
  <span id="freeText6747105205675028035" style="display:none">Oh my goodness I loved this book for so many reasons!<br />You can tell the author took her time writing it, because the characters are well developed and there's an in depth and intricate (not convoluted) plot. I haven't read a crime/law type romance novel in a long time, and I'd forgotten just how much I love them! So all this to say, first off, I loved the story and the way it's written.<br />But what I really really REALLY loved was how real it was!! I'm weird. I want romance, I want suspense, I want hotness, and I want happily ever after. And I want it to feel real. Even if it's a totally out there storyline, I still like to feel like it could happen. This book was genius because the author took very real life situations, real life reactions and emotions, real life people, and told their story so you felt like you were peering in their apartment window (in a totally non creeper way). Kate and Derrick meet in such a cute and normal way. They begin dating. Like, dating as in 'go out on dates' dating. They take their time. Weird.<br />Written in 3rd person, you get to see each of their insecurities and the foibles in their growing relationship. And then life happens. Some of the bad stuff in life. The stuff you think you know how you'd handle, or how you'd hope to handle. But until you're thrust into that position, you don't know. Hearts and trust are broken, tainted. MY heart was broken. I cried. But they are human and they find the strength to understand and to forgive and to pick up the pieces as best they can. Kate is exceptionally strong and I think you will find her to be an inspiration as much a Derrick will. <br />By the way, this is the first in a trilogy. Of course there's a cliffhanger! How else would there be more books! And no way could this story have been told in one anyway! But get this one because book 2 is coming next month and you'll want to be ready!</span>
  <a data-text-id="6747105205675028035" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer11679182790069473328">Review for Tainted Bodies 5 Stars.<br/>Characters were well rounded everyday people. I loved this. I love the feeling you get when you read a book and you can relate to the characters.<br/>In this book we meet Kate Jackson who is working in a furniture store. She seems to have the same morning routine that includes stoping into the corner coffee shop daily on her way to work.<br/>One morning she meets Derrick Kane, at the coffee shop, when he uses this cheesey type of pick up skit with her.<br/>As the book goes on </span>
  <span id="freeText11679182790069473328" style="display:none">Review for Tainted Bodies 5 Stars.<br />Characters were well rounded everyday people. I loved this. I love the feeling you get when you read a book and you can relate to the characters.<br />In this book we meet Kate Jackson who is working in a furniture store. She seems to have the same morning routine that includes stoping into the corner coffee shop daily on her way to work.<br />One morning she meets Derrick Kane, at the coffee shop, when he uses this cheesey type of pick up skit with her.<br />As the book goes on we learn more about Kate's past and events from her childhood. And all the things she has had to overcome. We also learn why Derrick has commitment issues.<br />Together they help each other figure things out. But before they can get to that point certain tramatizing events happen. While these events take place I found myself wanting to slap Kate for choices she made. (Over time she fixes those choices.) And Derrick left me wanting to karate chop him in the throat for walking out in her time of need.<br />When the end came I was shocked. I was left wanting more. Needing more. I want answers. I can't wait until the next book comes out. Hopefully some of those answer will be in that book and I won't have to completely wait for book three. <br />The suspense of who did this is eating me alive!<br /></span>

<div id="review_846110498" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/846110498" />
    <a title="Night Owl Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/19886701-night-owl-reads"><img alt="Night Owl Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1536240047p2/19886701.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/846110498?book_show_action=true">Feb 05, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Night Owl Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Night Owl Reads" href="/user/show/19886701-night-owl-reads">Night Owl Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer846110498" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1324146539289686650">Kate Jackson is not living the life she anticipated... She is not working in the field she graduated college from, just listlessly floating through life having no idea what she truly wants to do with her life. <br/><br/>Living in the past doesn't help her cause either, letting things from her childhood continue to take over her adulthood. But then one day changes every thing. On her way to work she meets Derrick Kane in a local coffee shop in downtown D.C. <br/><br/>That day starts a whirlwind of a romance, leaving</span>
  <span id="freeText1324146539289686650" style="display:none">Kate Jackson is not living the life she anticipated... She is not working in the field she graduated college from, just listlessly floating through life having no idea what she truly wants to do with her life. <br /><br />Living in the past doesn't help her cause either, letting things from her childhood continue to take over her adulthood. But then one day changes every thing. On her way to work she meets Derrick Kane in a local coffee shop in downtown D.C. <br /><br />That day starts a whirlwind of a romance, leaving Kate to believe Derrick is the answer to all her problems, hoping he will be the one to mend the open wounds of her past. <br /><br />Just as she feels she can move on from her horrible past, a shocking crime forces Kate to learn how to deal with it herself, not letting her past invade her present and leads her into a mystery that only Kate can solve.<br /><br />This is a totally different book than what you are probably thinking. You will not find this book in the "After 50 Shades" section. It does tell us the about a couple and their whirlwind of a romance but there is no erotica or BDSM about it! <br /><br />You will love Derrick and Kate at the beginning but then things start to become fishy. You can tell Derrick has his secrets. They jump into a relationship so fast, but after sometime, you can see and feel Derrick is hiding things from Kate. <br /><br />This book is a crime-romance. There is hot sexy scenes, you can feel the chemistry between them, no doubt. But when Derrick lands himself in hot water, it all comes to a screaming hault. But Kate doesn't realize it is up to her to save him, not knowing she is the key to saving the man she loves. <br /><br />This is my first read by Sarah Robinson... But this is her second book. She contacted me via my page asking for an honest review. Tainted Bodies is the first book in what will be a trilogy. I did enjoy this book, it was a nice change to what I have been reading lately.<br /><br />This book will grab you right from the beginning. You fall for Derricks charm just like Kate does but then you will realize something is wrong. There are so many secrets and lies, you can't help but continue to read because you want to solve the mystery.<br /><br />You instantly want to scream at Kate, "Don't trust him, he isn't being honest with you." You will get that strange feeling like you know something is about to happen. But there is a second book in the works, so Derrick has time to redeem himself. <br /><br />Watch for book 2 and more of Kate and Derrick to come later this year! <br /><br />Thank you Sarah for letting me be a part of this! <br /><br />I give Tainted Bodies 4 out of 5 Owls.<br /><br />**Mature- 18+**</span>
  <a data-text-id="1324146539289686650" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_889799789" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/889799789" />
    <a title="Jill S (Love Affair With Fiction)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17646861-jill-s-love-affair-with-fiction"><img alt="Jill S (Love Affair With Fiction)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1524316366p2/17646861.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/889799789?book_show_action=true">Mar 23, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jill S (Love Affair With Fiction)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jill S (Love Affair With Fiction)" href="/user/show/17646861-jill-s-love-affair-with-fiction">Jill S (Love Affair With Fiction)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer889799789" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14889122998020419917">Sarah Robinson’s Tainted Bodies is a Crime Romance, a dark and heavy read that I could not bring myself to put down.<br/><br/>Romance, past traumas, sisterhood, secrets, betrayals and a horrific crime that occurs now—it doesn't seem like it would all fit together into a book that would leave ME wanting more. But it worked together flawlessly. It was real, raw and gritty—full of secrets, lies, mysteries and evasions which lead you up to a cliffhanger and breathlessly waiting for the second book in this ser</span>
  <span id="freeText14889122998020419917" style="display:none">Sarah Robinson’s Tainted Bodies is a Crime Romance, a dark and heavy read that I could not bring myself to put down.<br /><br />Romance, past traumas, sisterhood, secrets, betrayals and a horrific crime that occurs now—it doesn't seem like it would all fit together into a book that would leave ME wanting more. But it worked together flawlessly. It was real, raw and gritty—full of secrets, lies, mysteries and evasions which lead you up to a cliffhanger and breathlessly waiting for the second book in this series. Yet it also had another side to the book—the budding of a new relationship between Kate and Derrick, the close bond between sisters and the incredible chemistry between Kate and Derrick.<br /><br />One of the things I liked the most about Sarah’s writing was how utterly flawed and imperfect her characters were. Where usually we all dream about the knight in shining armor who swoops in and saves the day…let’s be honest we don’t see it every day. Derrick has flashes of the charming, dreamy, handsome, romantic man of our dreams and then there is that slightly mysterious, secretive commitment phobe side. Kate is dissatisfied at her job, yet is still there accepting promotions, all the while wishing and dreaming about something different. She is incredibly strong yet at the same time still broken inside. When she meets Derrick, their instantaneous connection starts off a relationship that truly excites Kate. However they are not exactly in the same page. <br /><br />I have to be honest that Sarah made me rethink how I rate books! Usually I reserve 5 Stars for books that I want to read over and over again. I can’t be certain that I want to curl up with Tainted Bodies again because the material is so heavy, intense and realistic (though I am not ruling it out!), but this book was so brilliantly written and has not left me since I swiped that last page that to give it anything less would be a gross injustice.<br /><br />I received a complimentary copy of Tainted Bodies from the author in exchange for my honest review.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14889122998020419917" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="Elle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14258639-elle"><img alt="Elle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1371483199p2/14258639.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/836880919?book_show_action=true">Jan 27, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elle" href="/user/show/14258639-elle">Elle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14258639-elle?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer836880919" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7675236474280248459"><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://meangirlsluvbooks.blogspot.com/2014/02/blog-tour-tainted-bodies-by-sarah.html'>http://meangirlsluvbooks.blogspot.com...</a><br/><br/>Tainted Bodies by Sarah Robinson is the perfect blend of romance, mystery, and heartbreak. This book cover is gorgeous and beneath it’s exterior is a story equally as stunning. I loved this novel from start to finish and the ending left me excited and anxious for the next book in The Photographer Series. <br/><br/>Kate Jackson is mindlessly going through life until a chance meeting with Derrick Kane. Sarah thoroughly builds their relationship as the pair is insepara</span>
  <span id="freeText7675236474280248459" style="display:none"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://meangirlsluvbooks.blogspot.com/2014/02/blog-tour-tainted-bodies-by-sarah.html">http://meangirlsluvbooks.blogspot.com...</a><br /><br />Tainted Bodies by Sarah Robinson is the perfect blend of romance, mystery, and heartbreak. This book cover is gorgeous and beneath it’s exterior is a story equally as stunning. I loved this novel from start to finish and the ending left me excited and anxious for the next book in The Photographer Series. <br /><br />Kate Jackson is mindlessly going through life until a chance meeting with Derrick Kane. Sarah thoroughly builds their relationship as the pair is inseparable and sparks fly. As their relationship unfolds, their connection is realistic and swoon worthy. The couple is down to earth, playful, and it’s the little gestures and time spent together that contributes to their growing foundation. I loved that Derrick came across as a normal guy. He didn’t need to throw around money and win Kate over with pomp and circumstance. Instead he pursued her with genuine charm and a desire to learn more about her on a deeper emotional level. To me Kate and Derrick seemed like a regular, real-life couple. It was refreshing to watch their courtship.<br /><br />As the plot progresses, filling my heart with flutters and hope for a happily ever after, there is a sudden, soul shattering twist. This unexpected turn left me breathless and with painful aches resonating in my heart. Relationships are tested, characters are destroyed, and everything I was certain of is now in shambles. I loved it. <br /><br />Immerse yourself in the first novel in Sarah Robinson’s The Photographer Series. Tainted Bodies is a mind trip full of heart-warming romance and heart breaking suspense. I cannot wait to get my hands on the next installment in Kate and Derrick’s story.<br /></span>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11308301167264545920">**4.5 Stars**<br/><br/>I typically do not read crime/romance books but I did enjoy this one.<br/><br/>Kate Johnson is living a normal life, with little to no excitement. She has a past that still troubles her some but does a great job at hiding it. When she goes to her normal coffee spot Derrick Kane enters her life and stirs up some excitement. <br/><br/>Derrick is hot, fun, and a little mysterious. He too has a troubled past.   <span id="freeText11308301167264545920" style="display:none">**4.5 Stars**<br /><br />I typically do not read crime/romance books but I did enjoy this one.<br /><br />Kate Johnson is living a normal life, with little to no excitement. She has a past that still troubles her some but does a great job at hiding it. When she goes to her normal coffee spot Derrick Kane enters her life and stirs up some excitement. <br /><br />Derrick is hot, fun, and a little mysterious. He too has a troubled past. You learn a little bit about his past and it gives you a understanding of why he the way he is at times. <br /><br />Kate and Derrick date for a while and you can tell by the way they are around each other they are in love but Derricks past gets in the way and it leaves Kate feeling a little insecure about their relationship at times. She is in love with him and determined she won't let it get in the way of their relationship.<br /><br />After an amazing weekend together the two go back home and a horrific crime takes place involving Kate. She must now help the police catch this sick and twisted criminal while trying to hold her relationship with Derrick together.<br /><br />The book started off a little slow for me but once it got going it sucked me right in. I ended up finishing in one sitting. Holy hell the reaction from Derrick about the crime just blew my mind. I won't say exactly how I feel because I don't want to ruin it for anyone. It does have a cliffhanger and I can't wait to find out what happens next.</span>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/828368395?book_show_action=true">Jan 19, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rozanne Visagie (Willow&#39;s Corner) " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rozanne Visagie (Willow&#39;s Corner) " href="/user/show/11308430-rozanne-visagie-willow-s-corner">Rozanne Visagie (Willow&#39;s Corner) </a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer828368395" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4289451266824593325">*ARC provided by author for a honest review. <br/><br/>This was an amazing read!(Little typos, but nothing serious). At first its all the details. Kate Jackson meets her perfect man, Derrick Kane. She is head over heels in love. They have their dates and just enjoys being in love and in each other's presence almost 24/7. We meet her sister, Annie, which is a lovable character. In the mean time Kate and Derrick is still much in love. Kate is decisive about her job, and what she actually studied for. But sh</span>
  <span id="freeText4289451266824593325" style="display:none">*ARC provided by author for a honest review. <br /><br />This was an amazing read!(Little typos, but nothing serious). At first its all the details. Kate Jackson meets her perfect man, Derrick Kane. She is head over heels in love. They have their dates and just enjoys being in love and in each other's presence almost 24/7. We meet her sister, Annie, which is a lovable character. In the mean time Kate and Derrick is still much in love. Kate is decisive about her job, and what she actually studied for. But she is appreciative of her job, it pays the bills. <br /><br />Then all of a sudden a surprising twist!! Something that I never expected to happen. I was really disappointed in how Derrick handled the situation, even though he explained to his best friend Brian, why he acted like that. <br /><br />Kate lost her trust in Derrick, but still decided to give him another chance, I wouldn't. But the heart wants what the heart wants. <br /><br />I am extremely excited to read the next book in the trilogy, and I can't wait. I have to know what happens next!! I would recommend this to anyone that likes reading romance with a brush of crime. <br /><br />Kate is a big Ellen DeGeneres fan and I found this quote, thinking of her. <br />“Accept who you are. Unless you're a serial killer.”<br />— Ellen DeGeneres</span>
  <a data-text-id="4289451266824593325" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_880172581" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/880172581" />
    <a title="Heidi Ryan" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/26149580-heidi-ryan"><img alt="Heidi Ryan" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1385862969p2/26149580.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/880172581?book_show_action=true">Mar 12, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Heidi Ryan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Heidi Ryan" href="/user/show/26149580-heidi-ryan">Heidi Ryan</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer880172581" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer729282734798902683">I would rate this book as a 4.5 if given the option. <br/>This is the first book in The Photographer Trilogy by Sarah Robinson. The main character, Kate Jackson, lives alone in Washington, DC and works for her "uncle" Lenny. He is a childhood friend of her father. The story begins with Kate walking up to a podium to give a speech to law enforcement. This hints that the story is going to be bigger than we know.<br/>Kate has suffered unimaginable trauma when she was 6 years old. Her mother used this for att</span>
  <span id="freeText729282734798902683" style="display:none">I would rate this book as a 4.5 if given the option. <br />This is the first book in The Photographer Trilogy by Sarah Robinson. The main character, Kate Jackson, lives alone in Washington, DC and works for her "uncle" Lenny. He is a childhood friend of her father. The story begins with Kate walking up to a podium to give a speech to law enforcement. This hints that the story is going to be bigger than we know.<br />Kate has suffered unimaginable trauma when she was 6 years old. Her mother used this for attention and her father calls her a liar. This shaped how she views life, and how not to trust that anyone will have your back when things go wrong. Her closest trusted family to her is her little sister Annie. Annie lives in New York City. They are very close because when they were young, their mother left them and their father turned to booze and died when Kate was in middle school. Annie is the only true family Kate has left.<br />She meets a man named Derrick one day at a coffee shop and soon they are dating. Derrick has a lot of baggage just like Kate does. Slowly we learn what all is holding him back from getting serious with Kate. After a few months, they go on vacation to a bed and breakfast in Delaware. Things go really well and her life is looking good. When they return, really horrible things happen to Kate and she has trouble dealing with the aftermath. She struggles to do the right things and just when she is at her lowest point, Derrick does something bad. How she reacts and deals with all of this is what the story is about.<br />I liked the different direction this story moves in. It is a breath of fresh air, completely different then other books of the same genre. This book has mystery, suspense, romance, intrigue. It is the whole package. I am looking forward to seeing how this trilogy plays out, and if you like a deeper story, but don't want gritty, this is a good place to start. Although the subject matter could be graphic, Sarah has written this as to not be so in your face like some books. I found myself getting frustrated with the characters, which for me is a good thing. When you start looking at the characters as if they are real, then the author has done a wonderful job of bringing them to life. This is a very interesting start to a very interesting trilogy, and I for one, won't miss a page. Check it out for yourself!</span>
  <a data-text-id="729282734798902683" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText10359555193028409466" style="display:none">Tainted Bodies (The Photographer #1) by Sarah Robinson<br />I received an ARC in exchange for an honest review.<br /><br /><br />	Kate Jackson and her sister Annie lost their parents at a young age and are left to take care of one another. Kate hasn’t decided what she wants to do with her life and in the interim sells office furniture by day. Once she meets Derrick Kane in a coffee shop things change quickly. Kate and Derrick are swept up in each other, but Derrick has some commitment issues, can Kate convince him to give her and love another shot? When an unthinkable tragedy happens, it shockingly rips them apart; will they be able to pick up the pieces?<br />	This book is full of suspense and drama! My heart broke for Kate, things were going so well and then it happened. And Derrick made me so mad I am pretty sure I started yelling at my kindle. I won’t go into details, because I don’t want to ruin it for anyone else. If you are a fan of Law &amp; Order and romance then I suggest grabbing this one. My only complaint was that the criminal content hadn’t started sooner in the book; the detective side of the book really grabbed my attention. I can’t promise a HEA in this one, but it will make your skin crawl and you will be dying to get your hands on the next book in the series. This novel is geared toward anyone 18 and over due to strong sexual content and extreme violence.<br />	Thank you to Sarah Robinson for the opportunity to read and review her book, I can’t wait for the next in the series!!<br /></span>

  <span id="freeText8335837104070471917" style="display:none">*An ARC of this Book Was Given To Me By The Author In Exchange For An Honest Review*<br /><br />This was a difficult review for me to write and I have mulled it over for a few days now and have decided that in reality I would probably give it 3 1/2 stars but with the rating system I always rate up hence the 4.<br /><br />This book tackles some difficult subjects and for me personally the way they were handled just didn't work. I am sure there are many people out there that will feel differently but I was asked to provide my honest opinion and that is how I feel.<br /><br />The overall story I found to be OK. Unless there is a major twist in the second installment I spotted the guilty party very early on and although I went into this knowing it was "part 1 of 3" I found the actual place it ended to be on the irritating side. There was no major cliffhanger, nothing really to hook me into wanting to read the next book.<br /><br />I found the main male character to be very irritating although I have to say it was a refreshing change from the "perfect" guy that almost every romance based book that I have read lately likes to portray.<br /><br />I think this is really a book people will be torn about. I am sure there are many reviewers out there that will rave about it but something just didn't work for me.<br /><br />V""V<br /><br />***Review has been done in conjunction with Nerd Girl Official.<br />For more information regarding our reviews please visit our Fansite: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/NerdGirl.ng">www.facebook.com/NerdGirl.ng</a> ***</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer871046816" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9114858336685636481">I almost didn't read this book because I knew of the material that was written in it, but I'm so glad that I did. Having lived through a similar experience as the main character in the book I struggle to read about it and not because I've lived it, but because I think authors sometimes romanticize it. Sarah Robinson did not do that. Her characters were very realistic. The pain they went through felt to me like real life pain. I found myself shaking my head and almost fist pumping the air in happ</span>
  <span id="freeText9114858336685636481" style="display:none">I almost didn't read this book because I knew of the material that was written in it, but I'm so glad that I did. Having lived through a similar experience as the main character in the book I struggle to read about it and not because I've lived it, but because I think authors sometimes romanticize it. Sarah Robinson did not do that. Her characters were very realistic. The pain they went through felt to me like real life pain. I found myself shaking my head and almost fist pumping the air in happiness that true facts were put into the book. It wasn't filled with fluff to work around the harshness of what happened. Sarah came right at you with what happened.<br /><br />Yes the book started out with the romance. She let you get to know Kate and Derrick, but I loved that. I am a detail oriented reader. I want the books I read to take me into the book just like I'm there where the author was when they envisioned it. This book did that for me. There were laugh out loud parts, parts where you wanted to slap them (sorry Derrick, but what you did was plain stupid), awwww moments, horrible moments that made you cringe and give you nightmares because they were written so well and the parts that just made you smile in this book.<br /><br />The supporting characters were great too. My favorite being Kate's sister Annie. We all have a sister, cousin friend, who is like Annie. Her spunk and fire adds a great dynamic to the story and progression of the book.<br /><br />Can't wait for book two because the ending was an OMG--seriously left me hanging moment...</span>
  <a data-text-id="9114858336685636481" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('lR0KdRAUQ7PKUCT3IyRmznMG/tcO+o+EM3owd2/g1QMM1TzQF64sVRorhehd/dWXIN/LHUKjhRb2pM7LlWUcqw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

Emma left her sultry Southern drawl behind, but not even her closest friends know that with it she left her heart.
